    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">“Leadership is changing. And that applies as much to software as it does to organizations. In a world moving faster than any single roadmap can keep up with, leadership is less about decisive control and more about enabling decisions to happen in the right places, at the right time, with the right mindset."

That’s the reality <a class="link" href="https://il.linkedin.com/in/yanivevenhaim?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Even-Haim Yaniv</a>, Wix CTO, and <a class="link" href="https://il.linkedin.com/in/aviran?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Aviran Mordo</a>, VP of Engineering, have faced while leading Wix through a decade and a half of massive growth — and now, into the age of AI.

Check out the 1st comment for the full article 👉

<a class="link" href="https://il.linkedin.com/showcase/wix-engineering/?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Wix Engineering</a></p>

  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">Hey, I’m <a class="link" href="https://il.linkedin.com/in/nikolai-botino-710739b6?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Nikolai Botino</a>, Senior Product Manager at <a class="link" href="https://il.linkedin.com/company/wix-com?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Wix</a> Stores 👋

Before the holiday rush takes over your feed, I’m taking over the Wix page with quick tips to help store owners turn shoppers into buyers.

Here we go 👇

✧ Most shoppers are on their phones, so make sure your store looks great on smaller screens. Keep fonts readable, colors easy on the eyes, and layouts clean. Test your store on a few devices to catch anything that feels off.

✧ Shoppers want options when checking out. Offer the most common methods your audience uses-credit cards, PayPal, digital wallets, even buy now, pay later. The easier the checkout, the fewer drop-offs.

✧ Your brand should shine through your store’s design - colors, fonts, and overall vibe. Don’t just list product features; explain how they help in real life. Use strong visuals - photos, lifestyle shots, short videos - to make your products relatable.

✧ Be upfront about shipping, returns, and refunds - it builds confidence. Follow up after purchases to ask for reviews, collect feedback, or reward repeat buyers with perks like coupons or loyalty points.</p>

    <section class="hidden-summary container-lined p-3 overflow-hidden babybear:p-2 papabear:mt-3 hidden max-w-[550px]" data-impression-id="conversion_prompt_guest_hidden_summary" data-id="conversion-prompt">
            <h2 class="hidden-summary__title text-xl text-color-text overflow-hidden break-words mb-2 leading-regular font-normal">
              Ne kaçırdığınızı görmek için hemen katılın
            </h2>

      <ul class="hidden-summary__summary-items">
